\mbox{\Hypertarget{classtools_1_1wallet2_aa81c51bec72e2bce69f762ce12017151}\label{classtools_1_1wallet2_aa81c51bec72e2bce69f762ce12017151}}

\index{check\_reserve\_proof@{check\_reserve\_proof}!tools::wallet2@{tools::wallet2}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{check\_reserve\_proof()}{check\_reserve\_proof()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{stdbool_8h_a1062901a7428fdd9c7f180f5e01ea056}{bool}} tools\+::wallet2\+::check\+\_\+reserve\+\_\+proof (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structcryptonote_1_1account__public__address}{cryptonote\+::account\+\_\+public\+\_\+address}} \&}]{address,  }\item[{std\+::string\+\_\+view}]{message,  }\item[{std\+::string\+\_\+view}]{sig\+\_\+str,  }\item[{uint64\+\_\+t \&}]{total,  }\item[{uint64\+\_\+t \&}]{spent }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Verifies a proof of reserve. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em address} & The signer\textquotesingle{}s address \\
\hline
{\em message} & Challenge message used for signing \\
\hline
{\em sig\+\_\+str} & Signature string \\
\hline
{\em total} & \mbox{[}O\+UT\mbox{]} the sum of funds included in the signature \\
\hline
{\em spent} & \mbox{[}O\+UT\mbox{]} the sum of spent funds included in the signature \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if the signature verifies correctly 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{get\_reserve\_proof@{get\_reserve\_proof}!tools::wallet2@{tools::wallet2}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_reserve\_proof()}{get\_reserve\_proof()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::string tools\+::wallet2\+::get\+\_\+reserve\+\_\+proof (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::optional$<$ std\+::pair$<$ uint32\+\_\+t, uint64\+\_\+t $>$$>$ \&}]{account\+\_\+minreserve,  }\item[{std\+::string}]{message }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Generates a proof that proves the reserve of unspent funds. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em account\+\_\+minreserve} & When specified, collect outputs only belonging to the given account and prove the smallest reserve above the given amount When unspecified, proves for all unspent outputs across all accounts \\
\hline
{\em message} & Arbitrary challenge message to be signed together \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Signature string 
\end{DoxyReturn}
